### [166] [Feedback-Driven Rate Control for Learned Video Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20104)
*Zhiheng Xu,Xuerui Ma,Chunhua Peng,Hao Zhang*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种反馈驱动的率控制框架，用于学习型视频压缩，通过PI/PID闭环控制器实现目标码率稳定跟踪，并结合双分支GRU调整控制器优化帧级比特分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端学习型视频压缩虽然取得了良好的率失真性能，但率控制方面仍研究不足，特别是在目标码率驱动和预算受限的场景下。现有方法主要依赖显式的R-D-lambda建模或前馈预测，在视频内容动态变化时缺乏稳定的在线调整能力。

Method: 1. 在DCVC风格框架上构建单模型多码率编码接口，通过率失真参数lambda实现连续码率控制；2. 提出对数域PI/PID闭环控制器，根据目标码率与熵估计码率之间的误差在线更新lambda，实现稳定目标码率跟踪；3. 引入双分支GRU调整控制器，利用预算状态特征和因果编码统计信息细化基础控制信号，优化帧级比特分配。

Result: 在UVG和HEVC数据集上的实验表明：PI/PID控制器在DCVC和DCVC-TCM上分别实现了2.88%和2.95%的平均码率误差。结合调整控制器后，方法进一步实现了5.69%和4.49%的平均BD-rate降低，同时将平均码率误差降至2.13%和2.24%。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为学习型视频压缩提供了实用的解决方案，既能实现可控的码率，又能提高率失真性能，在目标码率跟踪和预算约束下的比特分配方面表现出色。

Abstract: End-to-end learned video compression has achieved strong rate-distortion performance, but rate control remains underexplored, especially in target-bitrate-driven and budget-constrained scenarios. Existing methods mainly rely on explicit R-D-lambda modeling or feed-forward prediction, which may lack stable online adjustment when video content varies dynamically.
  We propose a feedback-driven rate control framework for learned video compression. First, we build a single-model multi-rate coding interface on top of a DCVC-style framework, enabling continuous bitrate control through the rate-distortion parameter lambda. Then, a log-domain PI/PID closed-loop controller updates lambda online according to the error between the target bitrate and the entropy-estimated bitrate, achieving stable target bitrate tracking. To further improve frame-level bit allocation under budget constraints, we introduce a dual-branch GRU-based adjustment controller that refines the base control signal using budget-state features and causal coding statistics.
  Experiments on UVG and HEVC show that the proposed PI/PID controller achieves average bitrate errors of 2.88% and 2.95% on DCVC and DCVC-TCM, respectively. With the proposed adjustment controller, the method further achieves average BD-rate reductions of 5.69% and 4.49%, while reducing the average bitrate errors to 2.13% and 2.24%. These results show that the proposed method provides a practical solution for learned video compression with both controllable bitrate and improved rate-distortion performance.

</details>


### [167] [Seeing Further and Wider: Joint Spatio-Temporal Enlargement for Micro-Video Popularity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20311)
*Dali Wang,Yunyao Zhang,Junqing Yu,Yi-Ping Phoebe Chen,Chen Xu,Zikai Song*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: 提出统一框架实现时空联合扩展，通过帧评分模块进行时间扩展，构建拓扑感知记忆库进行空间扩展，在MVPP任务中超越11个基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微视频流行度预测方法在时空维度存在局限：时间上依赖稀疏短程采样限制内容感知；空间上依赖平面检索记忆库，容量有限且效率低下，阻碍可扩展知识利用。

Method: 提出统一框架实现时空联合扩展：1)时间扩展：通过帧评分模块从稀疏采样和密集感知两个互补路径提取视频帧的亮点线索，自适应融合实现鲁棒长序列内容理解；2)空间扩展：构建拓扑感知记忆库，基于拓扑关系分层聚类历史相关内容，通过更新对应簇的编码器特征而非直接扩展容量，实现无界历史关联而无存储爆炸。

Result: 在三个广泛使用的MVPP基准测试上进行大量实验，方法在主流指标上一致优于11个强基线，在预测准确性和排序一致性方面均实现稳健提升。

Conclusion: 提出的统一框架通过时空联合扩展，实现了对极长视频序列的精确感知，同时支持可无限扩展的记忆库，在微视频流行度预测任务中表现出色。

Abstract: Micro-video popularity prediction (MVPP) aims to forecast the future popularity of videos on online media, which is essential for applications such as content recommendation and traffic allocation. In real-world scenarios, it is critical for MVPP approaches to understand both the temporal dynamics of a given video (temporal) and its historical relevance to other videos (spatial). However, existing approaches sufer from limitations in both dimensions: temporally, they rely on sparse short-range sampling that restricts content perception; spatially, they depend on flat retrieval memory with limited capacity and low efficiency, hindering scalable knowledge utilization. To overcome these limitations, we propose a unified framework that achieves joint spatio-temporal enlargement, enabling precise perception of extremely long video sequences while supporting a scalable memory bank that can infinitely expand to incorporate all relevant historical videos. Technically, we employ a Temporal Enlargement driven by a frame scoring module that extracts highlight cues from video frames through two complementary pathways: sparse sampling and dense perception. Their outputs are adaptively fused to enable robust long-sequence content understanding. For Spatial Enlargement, we construct a Topology-Aware Memory Bank that hierarchically clusters historically relevant content based on topological relationships. Instead of directly expanding memory capacity, we update the encoder features of the corresponding clusters when incorporating new videos, enabling unbounded historical association without unbounded storage growth. Extensive experiments on three widely used MVPP benchmarks demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms 11 strong baselines across mainstream metrics, achieving robust improvements in both prediction accuracy and ranking consistency.

</details>


### [168] [Realistic Virtual Flood Experience System Using 360° Videos and 3D City Models Constructed from Building Footprints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20746)
*Tatsuro Banno,Koki Kawada,Mizuki Takenawa,Masatoshi Denda,Kiyoharu Aizawa*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: 提出一个结合360°视频与从2D建筑足迹自动生成的3D模型的洪水体验框架，无需依赖现有城市模型即可在真实场景中实现3D洪水可视化


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有洪水体验系统通常使用虚拟城市而非真实地点，且缺乏足够的光照真实感，限制了用户将场景与自身环境联系起来的能力。虽然360°视频能简单可扩展地复制真实场景，但有效的3D洪水可视化通常需要目标区域的3D建筑几何数据，这在许多地区不易获得。

Method: 提出新的虚拟洪水体验框架，将360°视频与从广泛可用的2D建筑足迹自动构建的3D模型相结合。通过将足迹挤出到合理高度，并将构建的模型与360°视频进行空间对齐，实现无需CityGML等预存城市模型的真实环境3D洪水可视化。

Result: 在日本北海道芽室町（易受河流洪水影响的地区）演示了该框架。用户研究表明，该系统增强了用户设想特定地点洪水疏散情况的能力，展示了其作为灾害风险沟通和教育有效工具的潜力。

Conclusion: 该框架通过整合360°视频和从2D建筑足迹自动生成的3D模型，解决了现有洪水体验系统缺乏真实感和依赖预存3D城市模型的问题，为灾害风险沟通和教育提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Virtual flood experience systems, which enable users to vividly experience flooding, are attracting increasing attention as effective tools for communicating flood risks. However, existing systems typically rely on virtual cities that do not correspond to real locations and often lack sufficient photorealism, limiting users' ability to relate scenarios to their own surroundings. Although 360° video-based virtual environments offer a simple and scalable way to visually replicate real-world scenes, effective 3D flood visualization in these environments typically requires 3D building geometry of the target area, which is not readily available in many regions. To address this limitation, we propose a new virtual flood experience framework that integrates 360° videos with 3D models automatically constructed from widely available 2D building footprints. By extruding footprints to plausible heights and spatially aligning the constructed models with 360° videos, our framework enables 3D flood visualization in photorealistic environments without relying on pre-existing city models such as CityGML. We demonstrate the framework in Memuro, Hokkaido, Japan, an area vulnerable to river flooding. A user study with local residents showed that the proposed system enhances users' ability to envision location-specific flood evacuation situations, demonstrating its potential as an effective tool for disaster risk communication and education.

</details>
